<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_3">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ca">venir</strong> (<i>first-person singular present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/vinc#Catalan" title="vinc">vinc</a></b>, <i>first-person singular preterite</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/vingu%C3%AD#Catalan" title="vinguí">vinguí</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/vingut#Catalan" title="vingut">vingut</a></b>)</span>; <i>root stress</i>: <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><span class="usage-label-accent"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Central Catalan">Central</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valencian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Valencian language">Valencia</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balearic_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Balearic Catalan">Balearic</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> /e/
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a></li></ol>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_5">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">venir</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a> <span class="mention-gloss-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move from one place to another that is nearer the speaker</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b>Viens</b> vivre avec moi en France.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Come live with me in France.</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">See <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/venir_de#French" title="venir de">venir de</a></i>.</span></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Conjugation_3">Conjugation</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Conjugation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r86705003" />This is a verb in a group of <i class="Latn mention nowrap" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/-ir#French" title="-ir">-ir</a></i> verbs. All verbs ending in <i>-venir</i>, such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/convenir#French" title="convenir">convenir</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/devenir#French" title="devenir">devenir</a></i>, are conjugated this way. Such verbs are the only verbs whose the past historic and subjunctive imperfect endings do not start in one of these thematic vowels (<i>-a-</i>, <i>-i-</i>, <i>-u-</i>).
</p>
<div class="NavFrame">

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_6">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">Inherited</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_Spanish">venir</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venio#Latin" title="venio">venīre</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Spanish">venir</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_9">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lad">venir</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Hebrew_alphabet" title="Appendix:Hebrew alphabet">Hebrew spelling</a></i> <b class="Hebr" lang="lad"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D7%91%D7%B3%D7%99%D7%A0%D7%99%D7%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ב׳יניר (page does not exist)">ב׳יניר</a></b>)</span><sup id="cite&#95;ref-Folkmasa&#95;1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Folkmasa-1"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#reflexive" title="Appendix:Glossary">reflexive</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a> <span class="mention-gloss-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move towards someone or something</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1982</b></span>, Enrique Saporta y Beja, <cite>En torno de la torre blanca</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=660dAQAAIAAJ">[1]</a></sup>, Editions Vidas Largas, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=660dAQAAIAAJ&amp;q=venian">page <span class="None" lang="und">71</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="lad"><b>Venian</b> de Sitchilya, pechkavan en la mar i traian sus pechka a Selanik.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>came</b> from Sicily, fishing in the sea and shleping their fish to Thessaloniki.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>2004</b></span>, Moshe David Gaon, <cite><span class="Hebr" lang="und">פואזיאס</span></cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=rpNiAAAAMAAJ">[2]</a></sup>, <span class="Hebr" lang="und">מכון מעלה אדומים בשיתוף עם מרכז משה דוד גאון לתרבות הלאדינו, אוניברסיטת בן גוריון</span>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9789659032242" title="Special:BookSources/9789659032242">→ISBN</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=rpNiAAAAMAAJ&amp;pg=PT17">page <span class="None" lang="und">17</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="lad">dirijir se <b>vienen</b> para el konvento.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b>came</b> to guide the convent.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Middle_French">Middle French</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Middle French"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_7">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_French">venir</a></i>.

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_10">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="frm">venir</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a> <span class="mention-gloss-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss">go to a specified location</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren">)</span>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Descendants_2">Descendants</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Descendants"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li>French: <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#French">venir</a></span><ul><li>Haitian Creole: <span class="Latn" lang="ht"><a href="/wiki/vin#Haitian_Creole" title="vin">vin</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="ht"><a href="/wiki/vini#Haitian_Creole" title="vini">vini</a></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r68481116" /></li><li><span class="desc-arr" title="reshaped by analogy or addition of morphemes">⇒</span> English: <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/venue#English" title="venue">venue</a></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r68481116" /></li></ul></li></ul>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_8">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_French">venir</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venio#Latin" title="venio">venīre</a></i>.

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Occitan">Occitan</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Occitan"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_9">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_Occitan">venir</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venio#Latin" title="venio">venīre</a></i>.
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Old_French">Old French</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Old French"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_10">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">Inherited</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venio#Latin" title="venio">venīre</a></i>. Attested since AD 881 (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sequence_of_Saint_Eulalia" class="extiw" title="w:Sequence of Saint Eulalia">Sequence of Saint Eulalia</a>).
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_13">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">venir</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a>; to <a href="/wiki/arrive" title="arrive">arrive</a>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>13th century</b>, Unknown, <cite>La Vie de Saint Laurent</cite>, page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gallica.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/btv1b9062154g/f8.item.zoom">10, column 1, line 2</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="fro">Quant Saint Lorenz i est <b>venu</b></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When Saint Laurence <b>arrived</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Conjugation_8">Conjugation</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Conjugation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r86705003" />This verb conjugates as a third-group verb. This verb has a stressed present stem <i>vien</i> distinct from the unstressed stem <i>ven</i>, as well as other irregularities. Old French conjugation varies significantly by date and by region. The following conjugation should be treated as a guide.
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_15">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="osp">venir</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a>
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b>between 1140-1207</b>, Anonymous (or Per Abbat), <i>Cantar de mío Cid</i> line 3668:<dl><dd><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="osp">Essora dixo el Rey <b>venid</b> uos ami compaña<br />(<i>modernized spelling</i>) Esora dijo el rey, venidvos (=veníos) a mi compaña</span><dl><dd>At that moment, the king said, "<b>Come</b>, both of you, to my company (=to accompany me)..."</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b>between 1140-1207</b>, Anonymous (or Per Abbat), <i>Cantar de mío Cid</i> lines 1943-1944:<dl><dd><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="osp">Con todo esto auos dixo alfonsso / q̃ uos <b>vernie</b> avistas do ouiessedes sabor<br />(<i>modernized spelling</i>) Con todo esto, a vos dijo Alfonso que vos vernié (=vendría) a vistas do hobiésedes (=hubieseis) sabor</span><dl><dd>With all this, (king) Alphonse said that he'd <b>come</b> to see you wherever you'd like</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Descendants_5">Descendants</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Descendants"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li>Ladino: <span class="Latn" lang="lad"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Ladino">venir</a></span>, <span class="Hebr" lang="lad"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D7%91%D7%B3%D7%99%D7%A0%D7%99%D7%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ב׳יניר (page does not exist)">ב׳יניר</a></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r68481116" /></li>
<li>Spanish: <span class="Latn" lang="es"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Spanish">venir</a></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r68481116" /></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Poitevin-Saintongeais">Poitevin-Saintongeais</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Poitevin-Saintongeais"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_13">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">Inherited</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_French">venir</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venire#Latin" title="venire">venire</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_16">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="roa-poi">venir</strong></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="References_5">References</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: References"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><span class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source">Piveteau, Vianney (<span class="None" lang="und">1996</span>), <cite>Dicopoitevin</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://dicopoitevin.free.fr/index.php">[3]</a></sup> (in French)</span></span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Spanish">Spanish</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Spanish"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Etymology_14">Etymology</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Old_Spanish">venir</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/venio#Latin" title="venio">venīre</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judaeo-Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Judaeo-Spanish">Ladino</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lad"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Ladino">venir</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Spanish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Spanish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA nowrap">/beˈniɾ/</span> <span class="IPA nowrap">[beˈniɾ]</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410" /><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display: inline-block; list-style: none; line-height: 1em; border-collapse: collapse; margin: 0;"><tbody><tr><td>Audio<span class="ib-colon qualifier-colon">:</span></td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><audio id="mwe_player_16" controls="" preload="none" data-mw-tmh="" class="mw-file-element" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="1" data-mwtitle="LL-Q1321_(spa)-Rodelar-venir.wav" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/8/89/LL-Q1321_%28spa%29-Rodelar-venir.wav/LL-Q1321_%28spa%29-Rodelar-venir.wav.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-transcodekey="ogg" data-width="0" data-height="0" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/8/89/LL-Q1321_%28spa%29-Rodelar-venir.wav/LL-Q1321_%28spa%29-Rodelar-venir.wav.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/89/LL-Q1321_%28spa%29-Rodelar-venir.wav" type="audio/wav" data-width="0" data-height="0" /></audio></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:LL-Q1321_(spa)-Rodelar-venir.wav" title="File:LL-Q1321 (spa)-Rodelar-venir.wav">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>

<li>Syllabification: <span class="Latn" lang="es">ve‧nir</span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Verb_17">Verb</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="es">venir</strong> (<i>first-person singular present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/vengo#Spanish" title="vengo">vengo</a></b>, <i>first-person singular preterite</i> <b class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/vine#Spanish" title="vine">vine</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/venido#Spanish" title="venido">venido</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to <a href="/wiki/come" title="come">come</a> <span class="mention-gloss-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move towards the speaker</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="es"><b>ven</b> aquí &#47; <b>ven</b> acá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>come</b> here</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="Spanish:&#95;orgasmo" data-lang="es" data-id="orgasmo"><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac label-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content label-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#reflexive" title="Appendix:Glossary">reflexive</a><span class="ib-comma label-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac label-brac">)</span></span> to achieve <a href="/wiki/orgasm" title="orgasm">orgasm</a>; to <a href="/wiki/cum" title="cum">cum</a>; to <a href="/wiki/ejaculate" title="ejaculate">ejaculate</a></li></ol>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading4"><h4 id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</h4><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=venir&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Usage notes"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Unlike the English verb "to come", which can signify movement towards the speaker, the listener, or another mentioned place, <i>venir</i> always references movement towards the speaker. To indicate movement towards the listener or another location, use <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/ir#Spanish" title="ir">ir</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>:
</p>
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="es">Él <b>va</b> hacia ti.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He's <b>coming</b> towards you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="es">¿<b>Irás</b> a la fiesta conmigo&#63;</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Will you come</b> to the party with me?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
